BEGIN

-----R0020-C0020----
SELECT round(abs(nvl(sum(ACCT_BALANCE_IN_AED)/1000,0)))  INTO V_R0020_AMOUNT_AED_RESIDENT  FROM CBUAE_BRF1_1_DETAILTABLE
